<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:признавать.html>признава́ть</a> (5878)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:признать.html>призна́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">priznátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ва́ть</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-vátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>

<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:признавать.html>признава́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">priznavátʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:признать.html>призна́ть</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to recognize <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">to acknowledge the existence or legality of something</span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span></li>
<li>to acknowledge, to see, to admit, to own</li>
<li>to find, to consider, to declare, to pronounce</li></ol>

<p><b><a href = vnd.unilang:приз.html>приз</a><span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span><a href = vnd.unilang:на.html>на</a><span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span>ва́ть</b>
</p><p><a href = vnd.unilang:глагол.html>Глаго́л</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:несовершенный.html>несоверше́нный</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:вид.html>вид</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:переходный.html>перехо́дный</a>,    <a href = vnd.unilang:тип.html>тип</a> спряжения <a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:классификация.html>классифика́ции</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:а.html>А</a>. Зализняка — 13b.      <a href = vnd.unilang:соответствующий.html>Соотве́тствующий</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:глагол.html>глаго́л</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:совершённый.html>совершенного</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:вид.html>ви́да</a> — <a href = vnd.unilang:признать.html>призна́ть</a>.

***признание.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:признание.html>призна́ние</a> (3117)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:признать.html>призна́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">priznátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-а́ние</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-ánije</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_2">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:признание.html>призна́ние</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">priznánije</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:признание.html>призна́ния</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:признание.html>призна́ния</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:признание.html>призна́ний</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>acknowledgement, recognition</li>
<li>confession, admission, concession</li>
<li>declaration <i>(e.g., of love)</i></li></ol>

<p><b><a href = vnd.unilang:при.html>при</a><span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span>зна́<span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span><a href = vnd.unilang:ни.html>ни</a><span class="hyph-dot" style="color:red;">·</span>е</b>
</p><p><a href = vnd.unilang:существительное.html>Существи́тельное</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:неодушевленный.html>неодушевлённое</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:средний.html>сре́дний</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:род.html>род</a>, 2-е <a href = vnd.unilang:склонение.html>склоне́ние</a> (<a href = vnd.unilang:тип.html>тип</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:склонение.html>склоне́ния</a> 7a  <a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:классификация.html>классифика́ции</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:а.html>А</a>. <a href = vnd.unilang:а.html>А</a>. Зализняка).
</p><p><a href = vnd.unilang:встречаться.html>Встреча́ется</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:как.html>также</a> <span style="font-style: italic;background-color:CCFFFF;cursor:help;" title="устаревшее">устар.</span> <a href = vnd.unilang:или.html>или</a> <span style="font-style: italic;background-color:CCFFFF;cursor:help;" title="поэтическое"><a href = vnd.unilang:поэт.html>поэ́т</a>.</span> <a href = vnd.unilang:вариант.html>вариа́нт</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:написание.html>написа́ния</a>: признанье.

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:признательность.html>призна́тельность</a> (20854)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:признательный.html>призна́тельный</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">priznátelʹnyj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ость</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-ostʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:признательность.html>призна́тельность</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">priznátelʹnostʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:признательность.html>призна́тельности</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:признательность.html>призна́тельности</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:признательность.html>призна́тельностей</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>appreciation <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">a just valuation or estimate of merit, worth, weight, etc.; recognition of excellence</span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span></li>
<li>gratitude, thankfulness</li>
<li>acknowledgment, credit</li></ol>

<p><b><a href = vnd.unilang:при.html>при</a><span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span>зна́<span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span>тель<span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span>ность</b>
</p><p><a href = vnd.unilang:существительное.html>Существи́тельное</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:неодушевленный.html>неодушевлённое</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:женский.html>же́нский</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:род.html>род</a>, 3-е <a href = vnd.unilang:склонение.html>склоне́ние</a> (<a href = vnd.unilang:тип.html>тип</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:склонение.html>склоне́ния</a> 8a  <a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:классификация.html>классифика́ции</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:а.html>А</a>. <a href = vnd.unilang:а.html>А</a>. Зализняка).

<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">при-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">pri-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:знать.html>знать</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">znatʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:признать.html>призна́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">priznátʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:признавать.html>признава́ть</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to recognize <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">to acknowledge the existence or legality of something</span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span></li>
<li>to acknowledge, to see, to admit, to own</li>
<li>to find, to consider, to declare, to pronounce</li></ol>

<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:признать.html>призна́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">priznátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ся</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-sja</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.

</p>
<ol><li>to confess, to admit

***призрачный.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:призрачный.html>при́зрачный</a> (8582)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:призрак.html>при́зрак</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">prízrak</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ный</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-nyj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:призрачный.html>при́зрачный</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">prízračnyj</span>)
</p>
<ol><li>spectral, phantasmal, shadowy, ghostly</li>
<li>unreal, illusory
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:призрачный.html>призра́чная</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:надежда.html>наде́жда</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>prizráčnaja</b> nadéžda</i> ― <span class="e-translation">delusive hope</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">при-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">pri-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-зыва́ть</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-zyvátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:призывать.html>призыва́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">prizyvátʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:призвать.html>призва́ть</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to call, to appeal, to summon
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:призывать.html>призыва́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:на.html>на</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:помощь.html>по́мощь</a></i><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>prizyvátʹ</b> na pómoščʹ</i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation"><b>to call</b> for help</span></dd></dl></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:призывать.html>призыва́ть</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:к.html>к</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:ответ.html>отве́ту</a></i><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">prizyvátʹ k otvétu</i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">to call to account, to bring to book</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>to call upon <i>(to)</i>, to urge <i>(to)</i></li>
<li>to draft, to call out, to call up</li></ol>

<li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru">призывание</span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">prizyvanije</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li>

<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:призыв.html>призы́в</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">prizýv</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ни́к</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-ník</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>

<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:призывник.html>призывни́к</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">prizyvník</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="animate">anim</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:призывник.html>призывника́</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:призывник.html>призывники́</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:призывник.html>призывнико́в</a></b>)

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:прийти.html>прийти́</a> (255)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*prijьti</i>. Synchronically derivable as  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">при-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">pri-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-йти́</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-jtí</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:прийти.html>прийти́</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">prijtí</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:приходить.html>приходи́ть</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to come (to), to arrive (at)</li></ol>

<p><b>прий<span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span><a href = vnd.unilang:ти.html>ти́</a></b>
</p><p><a href = vnd.unilang:глагол.html>Глаго́л</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:совершённый.html>совершенный</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:вид.html>вид</a>, непереходный,   <a href = vnd.unilang:изолированный.html>изоли́рованное</a> спряжение, <a href = vnd.unilang:тип.html>тип</a> спряжения <a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:классификация.html>классифика́ции</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:а.html>А</a>. Зализняка — ^b/b(9).     <a href = vnd.unilang:как.html>Также</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:существовать.html>существу́ет</a> устар. <a href = vnd.unilang:форма.html>фо́рма</a> деепричастия <a href = vnd.unilang:прошедший.html>проше́дшего</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:время.html>вре́мени</a> <i>прише́д</i>, <a href = vnd.unilang:употреблявшийся.html>употребля́вшаяся</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:преимущественно.html>преиму́щественно</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:в.html>в</a> XIX <a href = vnd.unilang:век.html>ве́ке</a>. <a href = vnd.unilang:соответствующий.html>Соотве́тствующий</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:глагол.html>глаго́л</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:несовершенный.html>несоверше́нного</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:вид.html>ви́да</a> — <a href = vnd.unilang:приходить.html>приходи́ть</a>.

***прийтись.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:прийтись.html>прийти́сь</a> (559)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Prefix <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">при-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">pri-</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">indicating action or motion towards a terminal point</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:идти.html>идти́</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">idtí</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to walk or go</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ся</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-sja</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">reflexive</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:прийтись.html>прийти́сь</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">prijtísʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:приходиться.html>приходи́ться</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to suit, to fit <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content"><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">po</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + dative, someone</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:сапог.html>сапоги́</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:прийтись.html>пришли́сь</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:нога.html>ноге́</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">sapogí <b>prišlísʹ</b> po nogé</i> ― <span class="e-translation">the shoes fitted well</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:приходиться.html>приходи́ться</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:вкус.html>вку́су</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>prixodítʹsja</b> po vkúsu</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to be to smb.'s taste, to be to one's liking</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>to fall (on a date)</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">impersonal</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to have to <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">+ infinitive</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>ему́</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:приходиться.html>прихо́дится</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:ждать.html>ждать</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">jemú <b>prixóditsja</b> ždatʹ</i> ― <span class="e-translation">he has to wait</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:знать.html>зна́й</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:приятель.html>прия́тель</a>: <a href = vnd.unilang:если.html>е́сли</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>я</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>тебе́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:это.html>э́то</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:сказать.html>скажу́</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>мне</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:прийтись.html>придётся</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>тебя́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:убить.html>уби́ть</a></i><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">znaj, prijátelʹ: jésli ja tebé éto skažú, mne <b>pridjótsja</b> tebjá ubítʹ</i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">listen, pal, if I tell you this, I’ll have to kill you</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">impersonal</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to happen (to), to have occasion (to)
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:удивляться.html>удивля́ться</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:не.html>не</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:приходиться.html>прихо́дится</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">udivljátʹsja ne <b>prixóditsja</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">one should not be surprised, there is no reason to be surprised</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">impersonal</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> <span class="use-with-mention">used in combination with various adverbs</span>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>ему́</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:прийтись.html>пришло́сь</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:тяжелый.html>тяжело́</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">jemú <b>prišlósʹ</b> tjaželó</i> ― <span class="e-translation">he has had a hard time of it</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">impersonal</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to number, to account (for) <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content"><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:на.html>на</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">na</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + accusative</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:четверть.html>че́тверть</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:весь.html>всего́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:экспорт.html>э́кспорта</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:приходиться.html>прихо́дится</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:на.html>на</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:нефть.html>нефть</a></i><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">čétvertʹ vsevó éksporta <b>prixóditsja</b> na neftʹ</i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">oil accounts for one-fourth of all exports</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">impersonal</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to be due
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:на.html>на</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:каждый.html>ка́ждого</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:прийтись.html>пришло́сь</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:рубль.html>рублю́</a></i><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">na káždovo <b>prišlósʹ</b> po rubljú</i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">each person had to pay a ruble</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">perfective only</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to be related (to)

<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:приказчик.html>прика́зчик</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">prikázčik</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="animate">anim</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:приказчик.html>прика́зчика</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:приказчик.html>прика́зчики</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:приказчик.html>прика́зчиков</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">historical</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> shop clerk, shop assistant, salesman <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">hired worker in a shop in pre-revolutionary Russia</span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:приказчик.html>прика́зчик</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:в.html>в</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:лавка.html>ла́вке</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>prikázčik</b> v lávke</i> ― <small>(please add an English translation of this usage example)</small></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">historical</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> steward <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">managing landowner’s manor in pre-revolutionary Russia</span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:барский.html>ба́рский</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:приказчик.html>прика́зчик</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">bárskij <b>prikázčik</b></i> ― <small>(please add an English translation of this usage example)</small></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">figuratively<span class="ib-comma">,</span> dated</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> someone who blindly follows and obeys his master</li></ol>

</p><p><a href = vnd.unilang:глагол.html>Глаго́л</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:несовершенный.html>несоверше́нный</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:вид.html>вид</a>, непереходный,  <a href = vnd.unilang:возвратный.html>возвра́тный</a>,  <a href = vnd.unilang:тип.html>тип</a> спряжения <a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:классификация.html>классифика́ции</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:а.html>А</a>.
